**How do assignments work?**
‚Ä¢ Head DJs or higher will be given assigned users to review. These reviews are a reflection of how you have done in the week.

‚Ä¢ The assignments are always anonymous exactly like who the review is written by.
Zane (278627940403773441) at Tue Jun 09 2020 07:34:12 GMT+0000 (UTC)
‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢
**How do I write a review?**
‚Ä¢ A review can only be written by Head DJs or higher. 

‚Ä¢ A review can be written by heading to the panel by clicking **here**. 

‚Ä¢ The section named overall is a summary of the week, start with how they‚Äôve done for this week and list positives. 

‚Ä¢ The section named improvement is an improvement or a next step. The improvement or next step is something that you‚Äôd like the assigned user to complete for the upcoming week or improve upon.
Zane (278627940403773441) at Tue Jun 09 2020 07:34:42 GMT+0000 (UTC)
‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢

**What is a review?**
It‚Äôs in the name, duh.
‚Ä¢ A review is a formal assessment for a staff member and is feedback on how a user has done in the week.
‚Ä¢ A review consists of the rating, content (includes positives + improvements for the upcoming week).
‚Ä¢ Reviews are always anonymous. 
‚Ä¢ If a user feels as if their review is unfair, management or higher can be contacted.

If you cannot DJ this week (15th - 21st), please PM myself so we can log that you are unable to DJ or we can arrange for your slots to be deducted for the week (i.e. 1 or 2 slots required).

Please note, if your reason is not valid enough you will still be required to complete minimums especially if you‚Äôre on trial as a Radio DJ.

If you can only complete 1-2 slots, then so be it: confirmation is required from a Head DJ or higher. 

If you FAIL to provide a reason for why you have not completed your minimums, you will be dealt with fairly and appropriately.

We are knuckling down as we gain 50+ listeners daily and we can not afford to lose our listeners.

**_This is not a chore, nor a task: it is something you enjoy and do as a hobby otherwise you would not be here._**
